294→    /**\n   295→     * Creates a new {@link FetchRequest fetch request} in preparation for sending to the Kafka cluster.\n   296→     *\n   297→     * @param fetchTarget {@link Node} from which that can be submitted to the broker\n   300→     */\n   301→    protected FetchRequest.Builder createFetchRequest(final Node fetchTarget,\n   302→                                                      final FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData requestData) {\n   303→        // Version 12 is the maximum version that could be used without topic IDs. See FetchRequest.json for schema\n   304→        // changelog.\n   305→        final short maxVersion = requestData.canUseTopicIds() ? ApiKeys.FETCH.latestVersion() : (short) 12;\n   306→\n   307→        final FetchRequest.Builder request = FetchRequest.Builder\n   308→                .forConsumer(maxVersion, fetchConfig.maxWaitMs, fetchConfig.minBytes, requestData.toSend())\n   309→                .isolationLevel(fetchConfig.isolationLevel)\n   310→                .setMaxBytes(fetchConfig.maxBytes)\n   311→                .metadata(requestData.metadata())\n   312→                .removed(requestData.toForget())\n   313→                .replaced(requestData.toReplace())\n   314→                .rackId(fetchConfig.clientRackId);\n   315→\n   316→        log.debug(\"Sending {} {} to broker {}\", fetchConfig.isolationLevel, requestData, fetchTarget);\n   317→\n   318→        // We add the node to the set of nodes with pending fetch requests before adding the\n   319→        // listener because the future may have been fulfilled on another thread (e.g. during a\n   320→        // disconnection being handled by the heartbeat thread) which will mean the listener\n   321→        // will be invoked synchronously.\n   322→        log.debug(\"Adding pending request for node {}\", fetchTarget);\n   323→        nodesWithPendingFetchRequests.add(fetchTarget.id());\n   324→\n   325→        return request;\n   326→    }\n   327→\n   328→    /**\n   329→     * Return the set of <em>fetchable</em> partitions, which are the set of partitions to which we are subscribed,\n   330→     * but <em>excluding</em> any partitions for which we still have buffered data. ConsumerRecords Processing Chain\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe Kafka consumer fetch request processing chain involves building fetch requests, sending them over the network, parsing responses, and converting them into ConsumerRecords. This flow is implemented in the Apache Kafka client library (clients module).\\n\\n## Request Building Phase\\n\\n### 1. Fetcher Request Initiation\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetcher.java`\\n- **Method**: `sendFetches()` - Synchronized method that initiates fetches for assigned partitions\\n- Calls `prepareFetchRequests()` to get the list of nodes and their fetch request data\\n- Calls `sendFetchesInternal()` to actually send the requests over the network\\n\\n### 2. Request Preparation\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java`\\n- **Method**: `prepareFetchRequests()` - Builds a map of Node to FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData\\n- Determines which partitions are fetchable (have valid positions and are not paused)\\n- Uses FetchSessionHandler to optimize requests using fetch sessions\\n- Handles read replica selection and availability checks\\n\\n### 3. Request Building\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java`\\n- **Method**: `createFetchRequest()` - Creates FetchRequest.Builder with:\\n  - Isolation level (READ_UNCOMMITTED or READ_COMMITTED)\\n  - Max wait time and min bytes configuration\\n  - Session metadata (for fetch session optimization)\\n  - Rack ID for preferred read replica selection\\n  - Topic IDs for proper version negotiation\\n\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/FetchRequest.java`\\n- Represents the fetch request to be sent to the broker\\n- Builder pattern for constructing requests with proper versioning\\n\\n### 4. Network Send\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetcher.java`\\n- **Method**: `sendFetchesInternal()` - Uses ConsumerNetworkClient.send() to transmit requests\\n- Registers response handlers for success and failure callbacks\\n- Uses RequestFuture to track response completion\\n\\n## Network Poll and Response Handling\\n\\n### 1. Network Polling\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ClassicKafkaConsumer.java`\\n- **Method**: `pollForFetches()` - Orchestrates the fetch polling process\\n- Checks if data is already available in the fetch buffer\\n- Calls `sendFetches()` if new fetches are needed\\n- Polls the network client with a timeout\\n\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerNetworkClient.java`\\n- **Method**: `poll()` - Handles network I/O and response callbacks\\n\\n### 2. Response Parsing\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java`\\n- **Method**: `handleFetchSuccess()` - Parses successful fetch responses\\n- Extracts FetchResponse from ClientResponse\\n- Uses FetchSessionHandler to extract partition data from the response\\n- Creates CompletedFetch objects for each partition in the response\\n- Handles partition errors and leader epoch updates\\n- Adds CompletedFetch objects to FetchBuffer\\n\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/FetchResponse.java`\\n- Represents the fetch response from the broker\\n- Contains partition data with records, error codes, high water marks, etc.\\n\\n## Record Buffering and Collection\\n\\n### 1. Fetch Buffering\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchBuffer.java`\\n- Thread-safe buffer for completed fetches\\n- Stores CompletedFetch objects as they arrive from the network\\n- Maintains order with support for paused partitions\\n\\n### 2. Completed Fetch Representation\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CompletedFetch.java`\\n- Wraps FetchResponseData.PartitionData from the broker response\\n- **Method**: `fetchRecords()` - Converts record batches to ConsumerRecord objects\\n- **Method**: `nextFetchedRecord()` - Iterates through record batches and filters records\\n- Handles record decompression and deserialization\\n- Tracks record offsets and batch information (leader epoch, timestamp type)\\n- Implements READ_COMMITTED isolation level by filtering aborted transactions\\n- Performs CRC validation if configured\\n\\n## Record Collection and Conversion\\n\\n### 1. Fetch Collection\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchCollector.java`\\n- **Method**: `collectFetch()` - Main entry point for collecting fetches from FetchBuffer\\n- Respects max poll records configuration\\n- Handles paused partitions by re-queuing them\\n- Initializes CompletedFetch objects and validates partition state\\n- **Method**: `fetchRecords()` - Calls CompletedFetch.fetchRecords() to get ConsumerRecord objects\\n- Creates Fetch objects with records grouped by TopicPartition\\n- Updates consumer position and lag metrics\\n\\n### 2. Fetch Container\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetch.java`\\n- Holds ConsumerRecord objects organized by TopicPartition\\n- Tracks whether consumer position was advanced\\n- Stores next offsets for each partition\\n- **Method**: `records()` - Returns Map<TopicPartition, List<ConsumerRecord>>\\n\\n## Final Consumer Records Creation\\n\\n### 1. ConsumerRecords Creation\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ClassicKafkaConsumer.java`\\n- Creates ConsumerRecords from Fetch.records() and Fetch.nextOffsets()\\n- Passes through consumer interceptors (ConsumerInterceptor.onConsume())\\n\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/ConsumerRecords.java`\\n- Public API container class returned to user applications\\n- Implements Iterable<ConsumerRecord<K, V>>\\n- Groups records by TopicPartition\\n- Stores next offsets for position management\\n\\n## Alternative Modern Path (FetchRequestManager)\\nFor async/newer implementations:\\n\\n**File**: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchRequestManager.java`\\n- **Method**: `poll()` -
